 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto">
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;1.01 </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On February&#160;20, 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> US, Inc. <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;T-Mobile&#8221;),</span> Sprint Corporation (&#8220;Sprint&#8221;) and the other parties to the Business Combination Agreement (as defined below) entered into Amendment No.&#160;2 (the &#8220;Amendment&#8221;) to the Business Combination Agreement, dated as of April&#160;29, 2018 (the &#8220;Business Combination Agreement&#8221;), by and among <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint, Huron Merger Sub LLC, Superior Merger Sub Corporation, Starburst I, Inc., Galaxy Investment Holdings, Inc., and for the limited purposes set forth therein, Deutsche Telekom AG (&#8220;Deutsche Telekom&#8221;), Deutsche Telekom Holding B.V. and SoftBank Group Corp. (&#8220;SoftBank&#8221;), as amended by Amendment No.&#160;1 to the Business Combination Agreement, dated July&#160;26, 2019. As previously disclosed, the Business Combination Agreement provides for <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Sprint to combine their respective businesses, on the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in the Business Combination Agreement (the &#8220;Merger Transactions&#8221;). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The Amendment extends the Outside Date (as defined in the Business Combination Agreement) to July&#160;1, 2020, and further provides that the closing of the Merger Transactions will occur on the first business day of the first month (other than the third month of any calendar quarter) where such first business day is at least three business days following the satisfaction or waiver of all of the conditions to the closing of the Merger Transactions (such date, the &#8220;Closing Date&#8221;). In addition, the Amendment modifies the commitments of the parties with respect to actions that may be required to be taken in order to obtain any remaining governmental consents or avoid an action or proceeding by any governmental entity in connection with the Merger Transactions, subject to certain limitations. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Pursuant to the Amendment, SoftBank has also agreed to indemnify <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and its subsidiaries following the closing of the Merger Transactions against (i)&#160;any monetary losses arising out of or resulting from certain specified matters and (ii)&#160;the loss of value to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and its subsidiaries arising out of or resulting from cessation of access to spectrum of Sprint or its subsidiaries (&#8220;Lost Spectrum&#8221;) under certain circumstances, subject to limitations and qualifications contained in the Amendment. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">Concurrently with entry into the Amendment, <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> SoftBank and Deutsche Telekom entered into a letter agreement (the &#8220;Letter Agreement&#8221;). Pursuant to the Letter Agreement, SoftBank has agreed to cause its applicable affiliates to surrender to <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> for no additional consideration, an aggregate of 48,751,557 shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock (such number of shares, the &#8220;SoftBank Specified Shares Amount&#8221;), effective immediately following the Effective Time (as defined in the Business Combination Agreement). Immediately following such surrender, Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank are expected to hold approximately 43% and 24%, respectively, of the fully diluted shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock, with the remaining approximately 33% of the fully diluted shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock held by public stockholders. The Letter Agreement further provides that if the trailing <span style="white-space:nowrap">45-day</span> volume-weighted average price per share of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock on the NASDAQ Global Select Market is equal to or greater than $150.00 at any time during the period commencing on the second anniversary of the Closing Date and ending on December&#160;31, 2025 (or, if the Closing Date is on or after May&#160;1, 2020 and SoftBank so elects no later than June&#160;1, 2020, $150.00 at any time during the period commencing on the second anniversary of the Closing Date and ending on the fifth anniversary of the Closing Date or $160.00 at any time during the period following the fifth anniversary of the Closing Date and ending on the sixth anniversary of the Closing Date), <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> will issue to SoftBank, for no additional consideration, a number of shares of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> Common Stock equal to the SoftBank Specified Shares Amount, subject to the terms and conditions set forth in the Letter Agreement. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">In connection with the foregoing arrangements, the Amendment provides for certain modifications to the percentage thresholds applicable to SoftBank&#8217;s ownership with respect to its director representation rights in the Stockholders&#8217; Agreement (as defined in the Business Combination Agreement) to be entered into in connection with the closing of the Merger Transactions (which modifications will no longer apply in the event that <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> is obligated to issue the SoftBank Specified Shares Amount). </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The foregoing description of the Amendment (including the modifications to the form of the Stockholders&#8217; Agreement) and the Letter Agreement is not complete and is qualified in its entirety by reference to the full text of the Amendment and the Letter Agreement, copies of which are filed as Exhibit 2.1 and Exhibit 10.1, respectively, hereto and are incorporated herein by reference. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>

<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The completion of the Merger Transactions remains subject to certain closing conditions pursuant to the Business Combination Agreement, as amended. <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Sprint currently anticipate that the Merger Transactions will close as early as April&#160;1, 2020. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

Such factors include, but are not limited to, the failure to obtain, or delays in obtaining, required regulatory approvals, and the risk that such approvals may result in the imposition of conditions that could adversely affect the combined company or the expected benefits of the proposed transaction, or the failure to satisfy any of the other conditions to the proposed transaction on a timely basis or at all; the occurrence of events that may give rise to a right of one or both of the parties to terminate the Business Combination Agreement; adverse effects on the market price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s common stock and on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s operating results because of a failure to complete the proposed transaction in the anticipated timeframe or at all; inability to obtain the financing contemplated to be obtained in connection with the proposed transaction on the expected terms or timing or at all; the ability of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint and the combined company to make payments on debt or to repay existing or future indebtedness when due or to comply with the covenants contained therein; adverse changes in the ratings of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s debt securities or adverse conditions in the credit markets; negative effects of the announcement, pendency or consummation of the transaction on the market price of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s common stock and on <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s operating results, including as a result of changes in key customer, supplier, employee or other business relationships; significant transaction costs, including financing costs, and unknown liabilities; failure to realize the expected benefits and synergies of the proposed transaction in the expected timeframes or at all; costs or difficulties related to the integration of Sprint&#8217;s network and operations into <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile;</span> the risk of litigation or regulatory actions, including the antitrust litigation brought by the attorneys general of certain states and the District of Columbia; the inability of <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</span> Sprint or the combined company to retain and hire key personnel; the risk that certain contractual restrictions contained in the Business Combination Agreement during the pendency of the proposed transaction could adversely affect <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> or Sprint&#8217;s ability to pursue business opportunities or strategic transactions; effects of changes in the regulatory environment in which <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</span> and Sprint operate; changes in global, political, economic, business, competitive and market conditions; changes in tax and other laws and regulations; and other risks and uncertainties detailed in the Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-4,</span> as well as in <span style="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#8217;s</span> Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> for the fiscal year ended December&#160;31, 2019 and in its subsequent reports on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-Q,</span> including in the sections thereof captioned &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; and &#8220;Cautionary Statement Regarding Forward-Looking Statements,&#8221; as well as in its subsequent reports on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> all of which are filed with the SEC and available at www.sec.gov and <span style="white-space:nowrap">www.t-mobile.com.</span> Forward-looking statements are based on current expectations and assumptions, which are subject to risks and uncertainties that may cause actual results to differ materially from those expressed in or implied by such forward-looking statements. <Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 2.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><U>EXECUTION VERSION </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AMENDMENT NO. 2 </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>TO
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>BUSINESS COMBINATION AGREEMENT </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This AMENDMENT NO. 2 (this &#147;<U>Amendment</U>&#148;), dated as of February&nbsp;20, 2020, to the BUSINESS COMBINATION AGREEMENT, dated as
of April&nbsp;29, 2018 (the &#147;<U>Original Agreement</U>&#148;), and amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1, dated as of July&nbsp;26, 2019 (&#147;<U>Amendment No.</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1</U>,&#148; and the Original Agreement, as amended by Amendment
No.&nbsp;1, the &#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;), by and among <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT></U>&#148;), Huron Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware
limited liability company (&#147;<U>Merger Company</U>&#148;), Superior Merger Sub Corporation, a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Merger Sub</U>&#148;), Sprint Corporation, a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Sprint</U>&#148;), Starburst I, Inc., a
Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Starburst</U>&#148;), Galaxy Investment Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Galaxy</U>&#148;), and, for the limited purposes of the covenants and representations and warranties set forth in the Agreement
that are expressly obligations of such persons, Deutsche Telekom AG, an <I>Aktiengesellschaft</I> organized and existing under the laws of the Federal Republic of Germany (&#147;<U>DT</U>&#148;), Deutsche Telekom Holding B.V., a <I>besloten
vennootschap met beperkte aansprakelijkheid</I> organized and existing under the laws of the Netherlands (&#147;<U>DT Holdco</U>&#148;), and SoftBank Group Corp., a Japanese <I>kabushiki kaisha</I> (&#147;<U>SoftBank</U>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RECITALS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS,
Section&nbsp;8.3 of the Agreement permits the parties to amend the Agreement by an instrument in writing signed on behalf of each of the parties and duly approved by the parties&#146; respective Boards of Directors (or comparable governing body) or
a duly authorized committee thereof; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the parties hereto desire to amend the Agreement as provided herein. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the representations, warranties, covenants and agreements set forth herein, and for other good and
valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged, the parties agree as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE I </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>DEFINITIONS AND TERMS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Definitions</U>. Unless otherwise specifically defined herein, each capitalized term used but not defined herein
shall have the meaning given to such term in the Agreement. Each reference herein to &#147;the date of this Amendment&#148; shall refer to the date first set forth above and each reference to &#147;the date of this Agreement&#148; or similar
references shall refer to April&nbsp;29, 2018. For purposes of this Amendment and the Agreement as amended by this Amendment, &#147;<U>Amendment Effective Date</U>&#148; shall mean the date first set forth above. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE II </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AMENDMENTS TO THE AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Amendment to Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3 of the Agreement</U>. Section&nbsp;1.3 of the Agreement shall be
amended and restated in its entirety as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Closing</U>. Unless otherwise mutually agreed in writing between Sprint and <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> the closing of the Merger Transactions (the &#147;<U>Closing</U>&#148;) shall take place at the offices of Wachtell, Lipton, Rosen&nbsp;&amp; Katz, 51 West 52nd Street, New York, New York 10019, at 9:00
a.m., New York time, on the first day of a calendar month, other than any month that is the third month of a calendar quarter (or, if such day is not a business day, the following business day), which such day (the &#147;<U>Closing
Date</U>&#148;)<B> </B>is at least three (3)&nbsp;business days following the day on which the last to be satisfied or waived (other than those conditions that are not legally permitted to be waived) of the conditions set forth in <U>Article VII</U>
(other than those conditions that by their terms are to be satisfied at the Closing, but subject to the satisfaction or waiver of such conditions). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Amendment to Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;2.4(a)(ii) of the Agreement</U>. Section&nbsp;2.4(a)(ii) of the
Agreement shall be amended and restated in its entirety as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SoftBank shall designate four of such 14 directors prior to the
Effective Time. Of such four designees, at least two of such designees shall be designated following consultation with DT and the independent directors of Sprint and shall qualify as an &#147;independent director&#148; under the listing standards of
NASDAQ and the applicable rules of the SEC, one of whom shall also qualify as the &#147;Security Director&#148; (or equivalent) to the extent required by the national security agreement among Sprint, SoftBank, the Department of Justice, the
Department of Homeland Security and the Department of Defense, or any successor or replacement agreement or arrangement that may be entered into in connection with the transactions contemplated hereby or by the Stockholders&#146; Agreement or the
Voting and Proxy Agreement; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Amendment to Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;5.1(a)(viii) of the Agreement</U>.
Section&nbsp;5.1(a)(viii) of the Agreement shall be amended and restated in its entirety as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">create, incur or assume any
Indebtedness for borrowed money; issue any debt securities or any right to acquire debt securities; assume, guarantee, endorse or otherwise become liable or responsible (whether, directly, contingently or otherwise) for the Indebtedness of another
person; enter into any agreement to maintain any financial condition of another person; enter into any securitization or factoring arrangement; or enter into any arrangement having the economic effect of any of the foregoing, except for: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(A)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Indebtedness under the existing (I)&nbsp;$2.0&nbsp;billion revolving credit facility under the
Credit Agreement, dated as of February&nbsp;3, 2017, among Sprint Communications, Inc., as borrower, JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A., as administrative agent, and the other parties thereto, as in effect on the Amendment Effective Date; and
(II)&nbsp;$4.5&nbsp;billion accounts receivable facility under the Third </P>

the receipt of the Governmental Consents as soon as practicable. The parties further agree that their agreement to use &#147;reasonable best efforts&#148; in this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;6.3</U> shall not require any party to propose,

not limit the parties&#146; respective obligations (A)&nbsp;to act in good faith and (B)&nbsp;in respect of each Specified Matter, in accordance with, and subject to, <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;6.3(d)</U> of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section 6.3(d) of the Agreement is hereby amended to delete clauses (i), (ii) and (iii)&nbsp;thereof

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:13%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i) &#150; (iii) any loss, cost or diminution in value following the Amendment Effective Date of an amount in the aggregate in
excess of the limitation (the &#147;<U>Specified Cost Limitation</U>&#148;) in connection with each matter (each, a &#147;<U>Specified Matter</U>&#148;), in each case as set forth on Part 1 of Section&nbsp;6.3(d)(i) of the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Disclosure Letter, measured on a net present value basis (except as otherwise provided in Part 1 of Section&nbsp;6.3(d)(i) of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Disclosure Letter), to <FONT

each of clause (A)&nbsp;and (B), in accordance with, and calculated pursuant to, Part&nbsp;2 of Section&nbsp;6.3(d)(i) of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Disclosure Letter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Section 2.3 (including Schedule A) of Amendment No.&nbsp;1 is hereby deleted in its entirety and has

consents to each and every restriction, limitation or condition of a type contemplated by Section&nbsp;6.3 of the Agreement and set forth in a written agreement executed and delivered by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> prior to the

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint, DT and SoftBank. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.5&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Acknowledgment relating to
Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;7.1 of the Agreement</U>. Without limiting <U>Article VII</U> of the Agreement, each party hereby acknowledges and agrees that as of the date of this Amendment, if the Closing were to be held on such date, (a)&nbsp;except
for and subject to entry of final judgment pursuant to the Antitrust Procedures and Penalties Act in <I>United States of America et al. vs. Deutsche Telekom AG et al.</I>, the condition set forth in Section&nbsp;7.1(b) of the Agreement would be
satisfied, and (b)&nbsp;except for and subject to the consent of the California PUC, the condition set forth in Section&nbsp;7.1(c) of the Agreement would be satisfied, in each case on the basis of the consents obtained as of the date of this
Amendment; <U>provided</U>, that the foregoing acknowledgement and agreement is made without prejudice to the right of each party to waive each such condition on the basis that entry of such final judgment and/or the consent of the California PUC is
not required in connection with the transactions contemplated by the Agreement or otherwise. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2.6&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Amendment to
Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;8.1(b)(i) of the Agreement</U>. Section&nbsp;8.1(b)(i) of the Agreement shall be amended and restated in its entirety as follows: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">if the Merger Transactions shall not have been consummated on or before July&nbsp;1,&nbsp;2020 (the &#147;<U>Outside Date</U>&#148;);
<U>provided</U>, that the right to terminate this Agreement pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;8.1(b)(i)</U> shall not be available to Sprint, if Sprint&#146;s or any SoftBank Party&#146;s, or
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> if <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or any DT Party&#146;s, material breach of its obligations under this Agreement, the SoftBank Support Agreement or the DT Support Agreement,
as applicable, has been the principal cause of, or principally resulted in, the failure of the Merger to be consummated by such time; </P>

Indemnification</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Effective from and after the SoftBank US Mergers Effective Time, SoftBank
shall fully indemnify <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and its subsidiaries (including the SoftBank Surviving Entity, the Surviving Corporation and their respective subsidiaries) and each of its and their respective successors and
assigns (each, a &#147;<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4 Indemnitee</U>&#148;) against and shall hold each of them harmless from (i)&nbsp;any and all damages payable to a third party pursuant to a final,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-appealable</FONT> judgment, and other monetary Losses incurred or suffered by any such Section&nbsp;9.4 Indemnitee (including amounts incurred or suffered by Sprint or any of its subsidiaries prior to the Closing
Date, in accordance with (and subject to) Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter) arising out of, attributable to or resulting from any third-party Action arising out of, attributable to or resulting from the matters set forth on
Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter, and (ii)&nbsp;the loss of value to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and its subsidiaries (including the SoftBank Surviving Entity, the Surviving Corporation and their respective
subsidiaries) arising out of, attributable to or resulting from any loss, termination, cancellation or other cessation of access to any spectrum owned, held, leased or licensed by, or otherwise made available to, Sprint or any of its subsidiaries as
of the Amendment Effective Date (any such spectrum, the &#147;<U>Lost Spectrum</U>&#148;) that arises out of, is attributable to or results from the matters set forth on Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i)(B) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter, which such loss of
value shall be determined in accordance with Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(ii) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter (the matters set forth in (i)&nbsp;and (ii) together, the &#147;<U>Specified Claims</U>&#148;); <U>provided</U> that until the aggregate amount of
all Losses for which indemnification is available under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4</U> for the Specified Claims set forth on Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i)(B) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter exceeds $200,000,000, SoftBank shall only bear 50% of
such Losses up to an aggregate of $200,000,000 of Losses. For clarity, if the aggregate amount of all Losses for which indemnification is available under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4</U> for the Specified Claims set forth on
Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i)(B) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter exceeds $200,000,000, SoftBank shall bear 100% of such Losses in excess of $200,000,000. Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4</U>, the maximum
amount of all Losses for which indemnification is available under this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4</U> for the Specified Claims set forth on Section&nbsp;9.4(a)(i)(B) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter is the amount set forth on
Section&nbsp;9.4(e)(i) of the Sprint Disclosure Letter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The obligations of SoftBank to
indemnify the Section&nbsp;9.4 Indemnitees for the Specified Claims pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4</U> shall survive the Closing with respect to any matter for which indemnification is claimed on or prior to the fifth (5th) year
anniversary of the Closing Date until the final resolution of such claim. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE III </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ADDITIONAL REPRESENTATIONS AND WARRANTIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Additional Representations and Warranties </U><U>of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Merger
Sub, Merger Company, DT and DT Holdco</U>. Each of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Merger Sub, Merger Company, DT and DT Holdco represent and warrant to Sprint and SoftBank as follows: (i)&nbsp;such party has all requisite power
and authority to execute, deliver and perform its obligations under this Amendment, (ii)&nbsp;the execution and delivery of this Amendment by such party have been duly authorized by all necessary action on the part of such party, and (iii)&nbsp;this
Amendment has been duly executed and delivered by such party and, assuming the due authorization, execution and delivery of this Amendment by the other parties hereto, constitutes the legal, valid and binding obligation of such party, enforceable
against such party in accordance with its terms, except that such enforcement may be subject to the Enforceability Exceptions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Additional Representations and Warranties of </U><U>Sprint, Starburst, Galaxy and SoftBank</U>. Each of Sprint,
Starburst, Galaxy and SoftBank represent and warrant to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Merger Sub, Merger Company and the DT Parties as follows: (i)&nbsp;such party has all requisite power and authority to execute, deliver and
perform its obligations under this Amendment, (ii)&nbsp;the execution and delivery of this Amendment by such party have been duly authorized by all necessary action on the part of such party, and (iii)&nbsp;this Amendment has been duly executed and
delivered by such party and, assuming the due authorization, execution and delivery of this Amendment by the other parties hereto, constitutes the legal, valid and binding obligation of such party, enforceable against such party in accordance with
its terms, except that such enforcement may be subject to the Enforceability Exceptions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTICLE IV </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>MISCELLANEOUS AND GENERAL </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">4.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Ratification; No Further Amendment</U>. Except as expressly amended hereby, all terms, conditions and provisions
of the Agreement shall remain unmodified and in full force and effect. This Amendment is limited precisely as written and shall not be deemed to be an amendment to any other term, condition or provision of the Agreement or any of the documents,
schedules or exhibits referred to therein. Any amendment or modification of this Amendment shall require the prior written consent of each of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint, the DT Parties and the SoftBank Parties. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">4.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Effect of Amendment</U>. This Amendment shall form a part of the Agreement for all purposes. From and after the
date of this Amendment, any reference in the Agreement to &#147;this Agreement&#148;, &#147;hereof&#148;, &#147;herein&#148;, and &#147;hereunder&#148; and words or expressions of similar import shall refer to the Agreement as amended by this
Amendment. The provisions of Section&nbsp;8.3 (Amendment), Section&nbsp;8.4 (Extension; Waiver) and Article X (General Provisions) of the Agreement shall apply <I>mutatis mutandis</I> to this Amendment, and to the Agreement as amended by this
Amendment, taken together as a single agreement, reflecting the terms therein as modified hereby. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-11- </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">4.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Entire Agreement</U>. This Amendment, Amendment No.&nbsp;1 and
the Original Agreement (in each case, including the documents, exhibits, schedules and instruments referred to herein and therein), taken together with the Confidentiality Agreement, the Roaming Agreement and any other agreement entered into as of
the date of, and with reference to, this Amendment by and among two or more parties hereto (as between such parties), constitute the entire agreement among the parties hereto, and supersede all prior agreements and understandings, both written and
oral, among the parties hereto with respect to the Merger Transactions and the other transactions contemplated by the Agreement and this Amendment. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B><U>Exhibit 10.1</U> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><U>EXECUTION VERSION </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">February&nbsp;20, 2020
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">12920 SE 38th Street </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bellevue, Washington </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Deutsche Telekom AG </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Friedrich-Ebert-Allee 140 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">53113 Bonn, Germany </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dear Ladies and Gentlemen: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Reference is made to the Business Combination Agreement, dated as of April&nbsp;29, 2018 (the &#147;<U>Original Agreement</U>&#148;), as
amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1, dated as of July&nbsp;26, 2019 (&#147;<U>Amendment No.</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1</U>&#148;) and Amendment No.&nbsp;2, dated as of the date hereof (&#147;<U>Amendment No.</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;2</U>&#148;; and the Original
Agreement, as amended by Amendment No.&nbsp;1 and Amendment No.&nbsp;2, and as it may be further amended from time to time, the &#147;<U>Business Combination Agreement</U>&#148;), by and among <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US,
Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT></U>&#148;), Huron Merger Sub LLC, a Delaware limited liability company, Superior Merger Sub Corporation, a Delaware corporation, Sprint Corporation, a Delaware
corporation, Starburst I, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Starburst</U>&#148;), Galaxy Investment Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#147;<U>Galaxy</U>&#148;), and, for the limited purposes of the covenants and representations and
warranties set forth in the Agreement that are expressly obligations of such persons, Deutsche Telekom AG, an <I>Aktiengesellschaft</I> organized and existing under the laws of the Federal Republic of Germany (&#147;<U>DT</U>&#148;), Deutsche
Telekom Holding B.V., a <I>besloten vennootschap met beperkte aansprakelijkheid</I> organized and existing under the laws of the Netherlands, and SoftBank Group Corp., a Japanese <I>kabushiki kaisha</I> (&#147;<U>SoftBank</U>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with the transactions contemplated by the Business Combination Agreement and as an inducement to the willingness of SoftBank, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> DT and their applicable affiliates to enter into Amendment No.&nbsp;2, and for other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and sufficiency of which is hereby acknowledged, the parties hereto agree
as follows: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.1&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Definitions</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Unless otherwise specifically defined herein, each capitalized term used but not defined in this
letter agreement shall have the meaning given to such term in the Business Combination Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For purposes of this letter agreement: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U>Acquisition Price</U>&#148; shall mean the value of the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">per-share</FONT> consideration payable in respect of shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock in the applicable Sale of the Company, determined as of immediately prior to the closing of
the Sale of the Company. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U>End Date</U>&#148; shall mean, if the
Closing Date is (i)&nbsp;before May&nbsp;1, 2020, then December&nbsp;31, 2025, or (ii)&nbsp;on or after May&nbsp;1, 2020 then either (A)&nbsp;December 31, 2025 or (B)&nbsp;the sixth (6th) anniversary of the Closing Date, in either case of clause
(A)&nbsp;or (B), as set forth in the SoftBank Election Notice. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U>Threshold
Price</U>&#148; shall mean, if the Closing Date is (i)&nbsp;before May&nbsp;1, 2020, then one hundred and fifty dollars ($150.00), or (ii)&nbsp;on or after May&nbsp;1, 2020, then either (A)&nbsp;if the End Date set forth in the SoftBank Election
Notice is December&nbsp;31, 2025, one hundred and fifty dollars ($150.00), or (B)&nbsp;if the End Date set forth in the SoftBank Election Notice is the sixth (6th) anniversary of the Closing Date, (I)&nbsp;one hundred and fifty dollars ($150.00)
through and including the fifth (5th) anniversary of the Closing Date and (II)&nbsp;one hundred and sixty dollars ($160.00) following the fifth (5th) anniversary of the Closing Date through the End Date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U>Sale of the Company</U>&#148; shall have the meaning given to such term in the
Stockholders&#146; Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(v)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U>Trading Day</U>&#148; shall mean any day on which NASDAQ
is open for trading and has a scheduled closing time of 4:00 p.m. New York City time; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:9%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(vi)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> VWAP</U>&#148; shall mean, for any
Trading Day, the trailing volume-weighted average price per share of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock on NASDAQ (as reported by Bloomberg L.P. or, if not reported therein, in another authoritative source mutually
selected by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and SoftBank) measured over the forty-five (45)&nbsp;consecutive Trading Day period immediately preceding such Trading Day. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.2&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Surrender of Shares by SoftBank</U>. SoftBank hereby agrees to cause its affiliates to surrender, convey,
assign, transfer and deliver to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> for no additional consideration, an aggregate of 48,751,557 shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock (such number of shares, the
&#147;<U>SoftBank Specified Shares Amount</U>&#148;) effective immediately following the Effective Time, it being agreed that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shall be entitled to take, and to direct the Exchange Agent to take, such
actions as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> or the Exchange Agent reasonably determine are necessary or appropriate to effect the foregoing surrender, conveyance, assignment, transfer and delivery effective as of such time, without
any further action on the part of SoftBank, SoftBank UK HoldCo or their respective affiliates; <I>provided</I> that SoftBank shall, and shall cause its affiliates to, execute and deliver any assignments, assurances, instruments or documents, and
take and do any other actions or things, as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> may reasonably request to accomplish or in furtherance of the foregoing. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.3&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Additional Shares Issuable to SoftBank</U>. If the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> VWAP, at any
time during the period commencing on the second (2nd) anniversary of the Closing Date and ending on the End Date, is an amount equal to or greater than the Threshold Price (such condition, the &#147;<U>Additional Shares Issuance
Condition</U>&#148;), then, subject to the remaining provisions of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U>, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shall promptly, and in any event within ten (10)&nbsp;business days following the
delivery of such documents as may be reasonably required by the transfer agent for the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock, issue to SoftBank or, at SoftBank&#146;s written request, an affiliate of
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-2- </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
SoftBank that is then a record holder of shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock (a &#147;<U>SoftBank Designee</U>&#148;), for no additional consideration, a
number of shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock equal to the SoftBank Specified Shares Amount (the &#147;<U>SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares</U>&#148;). Notwithstanding the foregoing, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(i)&nbsp;T-Mobile</FONT> shall have the right to withhold, and shall not be required to issue (whether upon the satisfaction of the Additional Share Issuance Condition or at any time thereafter), shares of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock comprising the SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares to the extent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> elects, in
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> sole discretion, in order to recoup any or all indemnity obligations in respect of Specified Claims then due and owing from SoftBank or any of its affiliates pursuant to Section&nbsp;9.4 of the
Business Combination Agreement, whether owed to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> or any other Section&nbsp;9.4 Indemnitee (the &#147;<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;9.4 Obligations</U>&#148;), with such shares of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock valued for purposes of this clause (i)&nbsp;at the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> VWAP as of the date of the satisfaction of the Additional Share Issuance Condition, and with
such recoupment to be effected by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> withholding a number of shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock that, when multiplied by such
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-</FONT> Mobile VWAP, equals the amount of Section&nbsp;9.4 Obligations then due and owing; (ii)&nbsp;without limiting the rights of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> under clause (i), the issuance of
18,000,000 of the shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock comprising the SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares (the &#147;<U>Pledged Shares</U>&#148;) shall be subject to and conditioned upon
(A)&nbsp;the delivery by each and every applicable affiliate of SoftBank to which the Pledged Shares are issuable hereunder a valid and binding pledge agreement, in the form attached hereto as <U>Exhibit A</U>, securing the Section&nbsp;9.4
Obligations (the &#147;<U>Pledge Agreements</U>&#148;), and (B)&nbsp;the completion of such other steps as are reasonably necessary to reflect the creation and perfection of the related security interest; (iii)&nbsp;if between the Closing Date and
(A)&nbsp;the End Date, the shares of T-Mobile Common Stock shall have been changed into a different number of shares or a different class of shares by reason of any stock dividend or distribution, subdivision, reorganization, reclassification,
recapitalization, stock split, stock equity split, combination, exchange of shares or any similar event (an &#147;<U>Adjustment Event</U>&#148;), then the Threshold Price (but, for the avoidance of doubt, not any dates or periods set forth therein),
the SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares Amount and the number of shares set forth in the foregoing clause (ii)&nbsp;shall be equitably adjusted, without duplication, to provide SoftBank (or, if applicable, the SoftBank
Designee) with the same economic benefit, if any, that SoftBank (or, if applicable, such SoftBank Designee) would have had the right to receive if the Adjustment Event had not occurred, or (B)&nbsp;the second (2nd) anniversary of the Closing Date, a
definitive agreement for the Sale of the Company is entered into, then, subject to the foregoing clauses (i)&nbsp;and (ii) (which shall apply to any consideration to which SoftBank (or, if applicable, the SoftBank Designee) may become entitled in
connection with the Sale of the Company pursuant to this clause (B)), if the Acquisition Price is equal to or greater than the Threshold Price, then <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shall issue to SoftBank (or, if applicable, the
SoftBank Designee) the SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares for no additional consideration immediately prior to the closing of such Sale of the Company, such that SoftBank (or, if applicable, the SoftBank Designee) shall
receive the applicable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">per-share</FONT> consideration payable in respect of each such share of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock in the Sale of the Company; and (iv)&nbsp;the Threshold
Price shall be reduced by the per share amount of any cash dividends or other cash distributions declared or paid on the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock between the Closing Date and the End Date. For the avoidance of
doubt, all shares of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> Common Stock issued pursuant to this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> shall be subject to the terms and conditions of the Stockholders&#146; Agreement and the Voting and
Proxy Agreement in the same manner as if such shares had been issued at the Closing without giving effect to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.2</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-3- </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.4&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>SoftBank Election Notice</U>. If the Closing Date is on or
after May&nbsp;1, 2020, then SoftBank shall, by written notice (the &#147;<U>SoftBank Election Notice</U>&#148;) to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and DT delivered no later than the Closing Date (<I>provided</I>, that if the
Closing Date shall not have occurred prior to June&nbsp;1, 2020, then the SoftBank Election Notice shall be delivered no later than June&nbsp;1, 2020), elect the terms set forth in either (but not any combination of) the following clause (a)&nbsp;or
the following clause (b): </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;an End Date of December&nbsp;31, 2025 and a Threshold Price of one hundred and fifty
dollars ($150.00); or </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:9%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;an End Date of the sixth (6th) anniversary of the Closing Date and a Threshold Price of
(i)&nbsp;one hundred and fifty dollars ($150.00) through and including the fifth (5th) anniversary of the Closing Date and (ii)&nbsp;one hundred and sixty dollars ($160.00) following the fifth (5th) anniversary of the Closing Date through the End
Date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.5&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Term and Termination</U>. This letter agreement shall continue in full force and effect from and
after the date hereof until the earliest of (i)&nbsp;the issuance of all SoftBank <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">True-Up</FONT> Shares to which SoftBank is entitled pursuant to <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> (and subject to the execution
and delivery of the Pledge Agreement(s) by SoftBank and/or its applicable affiliate(s), as applicable), whereupon <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> of this letter agreement (other than the last sentence thereof) shall forever terminate,
automatically and without any further action on the part of the parties hereto, and shall become void and of no force or effect, (ii)&nbsp;the End Date, if the Additional Shares Issuance Condition has not been satisfied as of such date, whereupon
<U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> of this letter agreement shall forever terminate, automatically and without any further action on the part of the parties hereto, and shall become void and of no force or effect, (iii)&nbsp;the consummation of a
Sale of the Company pursuant to which the Acquisition Price is less than the Threshold Price, whereupon <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> of this letter agreement (other than the last sentence thereof) shall forever terminate, automatically and
without any further action on the part of the parties hereto, and shall become void and of no force or effect, and (iv)&nbsp;the termination of the Business Combination Agreement prior to the SoftBank US Mergers Effective Time, whereupon this letter
agreement shall forever terminate, automatically and without any further action on the part of the parties hereto, and shall become void and of no force or effect. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.6&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Amendment; Waiver</U>. Any amendment or modification of this letter agreement shall require the prior written
consent of each of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> DT and SoftBank. A party hereto may (a)&nbsp;extend the time for the performance of any of the obligations or other acts of the other parties or (b)&nbsp;waive compliance by the
other party with any of the agreements or conditions contained in this letter agreement. Any agreement on the part of a party hereto to any such extension or waiver shall be valid only if set forth in an instrument in writing signed on behalf of
such party. Any extension or waiver given in compliance with this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.5</U> or failure to insist on strict compliance with an obligation, covenant, agreement or condition shall not operate as a waiver of, or estoppel with
respect to, any subsequent or other failure. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.7&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Miscellaneous</U>. The provisions of Article X (General
Provisions) (other than Section&nbsp;10.1, Section&nbsp;10.9 and Section&nbsp;10.14) of the Business Combination Agreement shall apply <I>mutatis mutandis</I> to this letter agreement. This letter agreement shall be binding upon and inure to the
benefit of the parties hereto and their respective successors, heirs, legal representatives and permitted assigns. Except as otherwise provided in this letter agreement </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-4- </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
(with respect to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> or DT only and, for the avoidance of doubt, without limiting any right of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> to
agree to or consummate a Sale of the Company), no party may directly or indirectly assign any of its rights or delegate any of its obligations under this letter agreement, without the prior written consent of the other parties; <I>provided</I> that,
without the written consent of the other parties, (a)&nbsp;DT may assign any of its rights or obligations hereunder, in whole or in part, to any Person (as used herein, such term shall have the meaning given to such term in the Stockholders&#146;
Agreement) that will be a successor to or that will acquire Control (as used herein, such term shall have the meaning given to such term in the Stockholders&#146; Agreement) of DT, whether by merger, consolidation or sale of all or substantially all
of its assets, and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(b)&nbsp;T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> obligations will succeed to any Person that will be a successor to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> whether by merger, consolidation or sale of all
or substantially all of its assets. Any purported direct or indirect assignment in violation of this <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.7</U> shall be null and void <I>ab initio</I>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1.8&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<U>Security Interest</U>. Without in any way limiting the effect of <U>Section</U><U></U><U>&nbsp;1.3</U> above,
SoftBank hereby grants to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> a security interest in all of its rights and interests in respect of the Pledged Shares under this letter agreement, as collateral security for the prompt and complete
payment and performance of the Section&nbsp;9.4 Obligations, whether such Section&nbsp;9.4 Obligations are owed to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> or any other Section&nbsp;9.4 Indemnitee; <I>provided</I> that the security interest
hereunder shall automatically terminate upon execution and delivery of the Pledge Agreement(s) by SoftBank and/or its applicable affiliate(s), as applicable. </P>

<TITLE>EX-99.1</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint Announce Amendment to Business Combination Agreement </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Companies drive forward toward closing the merger to become the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> as early as
April&nbsp;1, 2020 </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Bellevue, Washington and Overland Park, Kansas &#150; February&nbsp;20, 2020 &#150;
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) and Sprint Corporation (NYSE: S) today announced that they have entered into an amendment to their definitive Business Combination Agreement to create the New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> The Boards of Directors of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint have unanimously approved the amendment. The amendment has no impact on
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> previously stated outlook on the New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> synergies, long-term profitability and cash generation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A separate arrangement entered into by SoftBank Group Corp. in connection with the amendment will result in an effective exchange ratio of approximately 11.00
Sprint shares for each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> share immediately following the closing of the merger, an increase from the originally agreed 9.75 shares. This is a result of SoftBank agreeing to surrender approximately
48.8&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shares acquired in the merger to New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> immediately following the closing of the transaction, making SoftBank&#146;s effective ratio
11.31 Sprint shares per <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> share. Sprint shareholders other than SoftBank will continue to receive the original fixed exchange ratio of 0.10256 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shares for
each Sprint share, or the equivalent of approximately 9.75 Sprint shares for each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Immediately
following the closing, and after the surrender of shares by SoftBank, Deutsche Telekom and SoftBank are expected to hold approximately 43% and 24%, respectively, of the fully diluted New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> shares, with
the remaining approximately 33% held by public shareholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> has agreed to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-issue</FONT> to SoftBank the previously surrendered shares upon the achievement of certain stock price milestones by New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> during a specified measurement period, and
subject to certain additional terms, as outlined in the letter agreement that will be filed by each of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint with the SEC. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition, the amendment extends the &#147;outside date&#148; under the Business Combination Agreement to July&nbsp;1, 2020, and modifies certain other
provisions of the Business Combination Agreement as described in the companies&#146; SEC filings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Today&#146;s announcement is another significant
step forward toward finally closing this transaction! Throughout this journey, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint have been singularly focused on one thing: building a supercharged
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> that will offer U.S. consumers a broad and deep nationwide 5G network, more choice and greater competition. We are now on the threshold of achieving our goal.&nbsp;And did I mention how fun
it&#146;s going to be sticking it to Dumb, Dumber and Big Cable along the way? This is going to be epic!&#148; said John Legere, CEO of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;With today&#146;s agreement in place, we are now turning our attention toward our goal of closing this transaction and creating the New <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> as early as April&nbsp;1, 2020,&#148; said Mike Sievert, COO and President of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> and appointed CEO of the company starting on May&nbsp;1, 2020. &#147;We are on
the verge of being able to do what we&#146;ve set out to do from day one &#151; reshape a broken wireless industry </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
and create the new standard for consumers when it comes to value, speed, quality and service. The New <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> is literally going to change wireless for
good and now we&#146;re almost ready to get to the fun part: bringing our teams together, building this supercharged <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier</FONT> and becoming the envy of the wireless industry and beyond!&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Completing this step is yet another critical milestone in securing Sprint&#146;s future, and it brings us one step closer to closing this historic
transaction that has been years in the making,&#148; said Marcelo Claure, Sprint Executive Chairman. &#147;I&#146;m incredibly thankful for the perseverance and resilience of everyone that has gotten us to this point.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint combination remains subject to certain closing conditions. Additional information can be found
at www.NewTMobile.com. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">PJT Partners and Goldman Sachs are acting as financial advisors to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> Wachtell,
Lipton, Rosen&nbsp;&amp; Katz is providing legal counsel to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Deutsche Telekom. Evercore is acting as financial advisor to the committee of independent directors of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Latham&nbsp;&amp; Watkins is providing legal counsel to the committee of independent directors. Morgan Stanley is serving as a financial advisor to Deutsche Telekom. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Raine Group LLC is acting as lead financial advisor to Sprint. J.P. Morgan is also acting as a financial advisor to Sprint. Morrison&nbsp;&amp; Foerster
LLP is providing legal counsel to Sprint and SoftBank. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As America&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Un-carrier,</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc. (NASDAQ: TMUS) is redefining
the way consumers and businesses buy wireless services through leading product and service innovation. Our advanced nationwide 4G LTE network delivers outstanding wireless experiences to 86.0&nbsp;million customers who are unwilling to compromise on
quality and value. Based in Bellevue, Washington, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US provides services through its subsidiaries and operates its flagship brands, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Metro by <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile.</FONT> For more information, please <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">visit&nbsp;http://www.t-mobile.com.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Sprint:</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B>Sprint (NYSE: S) is a
communications services company that&nbsp;creates more and better ways to connect its customers to the things they care about most.&nbsp;Sprint served 54.2&nbsp;million connections as of December&nbsp;31, 2019 and is widely recognized for
developing, engineering and deploying innovative technologies, including the first wireless 4G service from a national carrier in the United States; leading <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">no-contract</FONT> brands including Virgin Mobile USA,
Boost Mobile, and Assurance Wireless; instant national and international <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">push-to-talk</FONT></FONT> capabilities; and a global Tier 1 Internet backbone. Today, Sprint&#146;s legacy of
innovation and service continues with an increased investment to dramatically improve coverage, reliability, and speed across its nationwide network and commitment to launching a 5G mobile network in the U.S. You can learn more and visit Sprint at
www.sprint.com or www.facebook.com/sprint and www.twitter.com/sprint. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Important Additional Information </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with the proposed transaction, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc.
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(&#147;T-Mobile&#148;)</FONT> has filed a registration statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4</FONT> (File <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">No.&nbsp;333-226435),</FONT> which was declared effective by
the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) on October&nbsp;29, 2018, and which contains a joint consent solicitation statement of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint Corporation (&#147;Sprint&#148;),
that also constitutes a prospectus of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> (the &#147;joint consent solicitation statement/prospectus&#148;), and each party will file other documents regarding the proposed transaction with the SEC.
INVESTORS AND SECURITY HOLDERS ARE URGED TO READ THE JOINT CONSENT SOLICITATION STATEMENT/PROSPECTUS AND OTHER RELEVANT DOCUMENTS FILED WITH THE SEC WHEN THEY BECOME AVAILABLE BECAUSE THEY WILL CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION. The documents filed by <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> may be obtained free of charge at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> website, at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">www.t-mobile.com,</FONT> or at the SEC&#146;s website, at www.sec.gov,
or from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> by requesting them by mail at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> US, Inc., Investor Relations, 1 Park Avenue, 14th Floor, New York, NY 10016, or by telephone at <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">212-358-3210.</FONT></FONT> The documents filed by Sprint may be obtained free of charge at Sprint&#146;s website, at www.sprint.com, or at the SEC&#146;s website, at www.sec.gov, or from
Sprint by requesting them by mail at Sprint Corporation, Shareholder Relations, 6200 Sprint Parkway, Mailstop KSOPHF0302-3B679, Overland Park, Kansas 66251, or by telephone at
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">913-794-1091.</FONT></FONT> </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>No Offer or Solicitation</B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B></B>This communication shall not constitute an offer to sell or the solicitation of an offer to buy any securities, nor shall there be any sale of
securities in any jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under the securities laws of any such jurisdiction. No offering of securities shall be made except by means of a
prospectus meeting the requirements of Section&nbsp;10 of the U.S. Securities Act of 1933, as amended. <B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cautionary Statement Regarding
Forward-Looking Statements </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This communication contains certain forward-looking statements concerning
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint and the proposed transaction between <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint. All statements other than statements of fact, including information concerning future results,
are forward-looking statements. These forward-looking statements are generally identified by the words &#147;anticipate,&#148; &#147;believe,&#148; &#147;estimate,&#148; &#147;expect,&#148; &#147;intend,&#148; &#147;may,&#148; &#147;could&#148; or
similar expressions. Such forward-looking statements include, but are not limited to, statements about the benefits of the proposed transaction, including anticipated future financial and operating results, synergies, accretion and growth rates, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s,</FONT> Sprint&#146;s and the combined company&#146;s plans, objectives, expectations and intentions, and the expected timing of completion of the proposed transaction. There are several factors which could
cause actual plans and results to differ materially from those expressed or implied in forward-looking statements. Such factors include, but are not limited to, the failure to obtain, or delays in obtaining, required regulatory approvals, and the
risk that such approvals may result in the imposition of conditions that could adversely affect the combined company or the expected benefits of the proposed transaction, or the failure to satisfy any of the other conditions to the proposed
transaction on a timely basis or at all; the occurrence of events that may give rise to a right of one or both of the parties to terminate the business combination agreement; adverse effects on the market price of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s common stock and on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s operating results because of a failure to complete the proposed transaction in the
anticipated timeframe or at all; inability to obtain the financing contemplated to be obtained in connection with the proposed transaction on the expected terms or timing or at all; the ability of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT>
Sprint and the combined company to make payments on debt or to repay existing or future indebtedness when due or to comply with the covenants contained therein; adverse changes in the ratings of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s debt securities or adverse conditions in the credit markets; negative effects of the announcement, pendency or consummation of the transaction on the market price of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s common stock and on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s operating results, including as a result of changes in key customer, supplier, employee
or other business relationships; significant transaction costs, including financing costs, and unknown liabilities; failure to realize the expected benefits and synergies of the proposed transaction in the expected timeframes or at all; costs or
difficulties related to the integration of Sprint&#146;s network and operations into <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile;</FONT> the risk of litigation or regulatory actions, including the antitrust litigation brought by the attorneys general
of thirteen states and the District of Columbia; the inability of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile,</FONT> Sprint or the combined company to retain and hire key personnel; the risk that certain contractual restrictions contained in the
business combination agreement during the pendency of the proposed transaction could adversely affect <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> or Sprint&#146;s ability to pursue business opportunities or strategic transactions;
effects of changes in the regulatory environment in which <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint operate; changes in global, political, economic, business, competitive and market conditions; changes in tax and other laws and
regulations; and other risks and uncertainties detailed in the Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4,</FONT> as well as in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile&#146;s</FONT> Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT>
for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2019 and in its subsequent reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q,</FONT> including in the sections thereof captioned &#147;Risk Factors&#148; and &#147;Cautionary Statement Regarding
Forward-Looking Statements,&#148; as well as in its subsequent reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> all of which are filed with the SEC and available at www.sec.gov and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">www.t-mobile.com,</FONT> and in Sprint&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the fiscal year ended March&nbsp;31, 2019 and in its subsequent reports on Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q,</FONT> including in the sections thereof captioned &#147;Risk Factors&#148; and &#147;MD&amp;A &#151; Forward-Looking Statements,&#148; as well as in its subsequent reports on Form
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> all of which are filed with the SEC and available at www.sec.gov and www.sprint.com. Forward-looking statements are based on current expectations and assumptions, which are subject to risks and
uncertainties that may cause actual results to differ materially from those expressed in or implied by such forward-looking statements. Given these risks and uncertainties, persons reading this communication are cautioned not to place undue reliance
on such forward-looking statements. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">T-Mobile</FONT> and Sprint assume no obligation to update or revise the information contained in this communication (whether as a result of new information, future events or
otherwise), except as required by applicable law. </P>
